# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="535a9-102">Membri obsoleti in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="535a9-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
